                                 when available.  The STDN-73 coordinate system has been                  
                                                                                                          
                                 re-defined so that all STDN-73 geocentric cartesian coordinates          
                                                                                                          
                                 are identical to WGS-84 geocentric cartesian coordinates.                
                                                                                                          


    SECT. B: FLAGS & FOOTNOTES USED THROUGHOUT LISTING








              %         Station deactivated or in caretaker status

         SECT. C: STATION ACRONYM SUFFIX LIST


              -A:  USB30: 9 METER, X-Y E-W

              -B:  ATSR S-BD RELAY

              -C:  CAMERA OR OPTICAL

              -D:  DEEP SPACE, RADIO TELESCOPES AND VLBI

              -E:  TLM 26 METER, X-Y PARABOLIC

              -F:  C-BD: FPS-16, MPS-36, CAPRI, TRADEX, TACAN

              -G:  GRARR S-BD

              -I:  RANGE/VALIDATION

              -J:  TDRSS BILATERATION RANGING TRANSPONDER

              -K:  K-BD

              -L:  LASERS

              -M:  INTERFEROMETERS OR MINITRACKS

              -P:  LAUNCH PADS, RUNWAYS, MPS LANDING STATIONS

              -Q:  C-BD: FPQ SERIES, TPQ-18, ALCOR

              -R:  ATSR AND TLM

              -S:  SRE, USB 4 METER, S-BD TLM

              -T:  C-BD: TPQ-18

              -U:  TDRS SATELLITE

              -V:  VHF: GRARR, SATAN(TX+RX)

              -X:  SRE-VHF: SATAN(TX), TLM

              -Y:  SRE-VHF: SATAN(RX), TLM; AIRCRAFT

              -Z:  SRE-VHF: SATAN(TX), SCAMP(TX), UHF, TLM, ALTA IR

              -3:  USB30: 6, 9, 26 METER, X-Y N-S

              -4:  TLM 12 METER & X-Y PARABOLIC

              -8:  USB85: 26 METER, X-Y E-W

              -9:  DOPPLER & GEOCEIVER

              -$:  SECOR
